          function setNull(obj){obj.value="";}function SendFilterSubmitPrice(){msg=$("#errormsg");pfrom=$("#minfitterprice").val();pto=$("#maxfitterprice").val();if(isNaN(pfrom)){alert(msg.data("from"));return;}if(pfrom==0 &amp;&amp; pto==0){alert(msg.data("error"));return;}if(isNaN(pto)){alert(msg.data("to"));return;}pfrom=parseFloat(pfrom);pto=parseFloat(pto);if(pto&lt;pfrom){alert(msg.data("greater"));return;}window.location.href="http://www.tinydeal.com/products_new.html?disp_order=6&amp;is_input=1&amp;scPath=1&amp;pfrom="+($('#minfitterprice').val())+"&amp;pto="+($('#maxfitterprice').val());}

       <script>
        (function(){
		
		var self = $("#mod_tagList");
		
		// edit by Simon for Ticket #3820
		if ( window.location.search.search(/main_page\=ws_search_result/g) !== -1 ) {
			self.find('.tag-list').not('.price-list').each(function () {
				$(this).data('height', $(this).height());
				var h = $(this).find('.tag-icon').length == 0 ? 29 : 45;
				if ($(this).height() &gt; h) {
					$(this).css('height', h).find('.showOn').removeClass('showOff').show();
				}
			});
		}
		

		self.find('.showOn').on('click', function () {
			if (!$(this).hasClass('showOff')) {
				$(this).addClass('showOff');
				var ah = $(this).closest('.tag-list').css('height','auto').height();
				$(this).closest('.tag-list').height(29).stop(true,false).animate({
					height : ah
				});
			} else {
				$(this).removeClass('showOff');
				$(this).closest('.tag-list').animate({
					height : 29
				});
			}
		});
		self.css('visibility', 'visible').find('.more').hide();
		self.find('.moreFt .btn-more').click(function () {
			if (!$(this).children('s').hasClass('down')) {
				$(this).children('s').addClass('down');
				$('.filter &gt; .more').slideDown('fast', 'linear');
			} else {
				$(this).children('s').removeClass('down');
				$('.filter &gt; .more').slideUp('fast', 'linear');
			}
		});
            if ( self.find('div.more a.checkStyle').length &gt; 0 ) {
                self.find('.moreFt .btn-more').trigger('click');
            }
})();
       </script>
